Sanskс╣Ыt</lang> (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>kva hariRakAnAM jIvitaM cA<srs />tilolaM kva ca vajra-sArAH SarAs te</s>, тАШwhere is the frail existence, of fawns and where are thy adamantine arrows?тАЩ, <ls>┼Ъak. i, 10</ls>); in later literature, however, the first <s>ca</s> is more usually omitted (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>ahaM tvaM ca</s>), and when more than two things are enumerated only one <s>ca</s> is often found (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>tejasA yaSasA lakzmyA sTityA ca parayA</s>, тАШin glory, in fame, in beauty, and in high positionтАЩ, <ls>Nal. xii, 6</ls>); elsewhere, when more than two things are enumerated, <s>ca</s> is placed after some and omitted after others (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>fRa-dAtA ca vEdyaS ca Srotriyo nadI</s>, тАШthe payer of a debt and a physician [and] a <ns>Br─Бhman</ns> [and] a riverтАЩ, <ls>Hit. i, 4, 55</ls>); in <lang>Ved.</lang> and even in <lang>class. Sanskс╣Ыt</lang> [<ls>Mn. iii, 20</ls>; <ls n=\"Mn.\">ix, 322</ls>; <ls>Hit.</ls>], when the double <s>ca</s> would generally be used, the second may occasionally be omitted (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>indraS ca soma</s>, тАШboth <s1 slp1=\"indra\">Indra</s1> [and thou] <s1 slp1=\"soma\">Soma</s1>тАЩ, <ls>RV. vii, 104, 25</ls>; <s>durBedyaS cA<srs />SusaMDeyaH</s>, тАШboth difficult to be divided [and] quickly unitedтАЩ, <ls>Hit. i</ls>); with lexicographers <s>ca</s> may imply a reference to certain other words which are not expressed (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>kamaRqalO ca karakaH</s>, тАШthe word <s>karaka</s> has the meaning тАШpitcherтАЩ and other meaningsтАЩ); sometimes <s>ca</s> is = <s>eva</s>, even, indeed, certainly, just (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>su-cintitaM cO<srs />zaDaM na nAma-mAtreRa karoty arogam</s>, тАШeven a well-devised remedy does not cure a disease by its mere nameтАЩ, <ls>Hit.</ls>; <s>yAvanta eva te tAvAMSca saH</s>, тАШas great as they [were] just so great was heтАЩ, <ls>Ragh. xii, 45</ls>); occasionally <s>ca</s> is disjunctive, тАШbutтАЩ, тАШon the contraryтАЩ, тАШon the other handтАЩ, тАШyetтАЩ, тАШneverthelessтАЩ (<s>varam AdyO na cA<srs />ntimaH</s>, тАШbetter the two first but not the lastтАЩ, <ls>Hit.</ls> <pb n=\"380,2\" />; <s>SAntam idam ASrama-padaM sPurati ca bAhuH</s>, тАШthis hermitage is tranquil yet my arm throbsтАЩ, <ls>┼Ъak. i, 15</ls>); <s>ca-ca</s>, though-yet, <ls>Vikr. ii, 9</ls>; <s>ca-na ca</s>, though - yet not, <ls>Pat.</ls>; <s>ca</s> - <s>na tu</s> (<ab>v.l.</ab> <s>nanu</s>) <ab>id.</ab>, <ls>M─Бlav. iv, 8</ls>; <s>na ca</s> - <s>ca</s>, though not - yet, <ls>Pat.</ls>; <s>ca</s> may be used for <s>vA</s>, тАШeitherтАЩ, тАШorтАЩ (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>iha cA<srs />mutra vA</s>, тАШeither here or hereafterтАЩ, <ls>Mn. xii, 89</ls>; occasionally one <s>ca</s> or one <s>na</s> is omitted (<ab>e.g.</ab> <s>na ca pariBoktuM nE<srs />va Saknomi hAtum</s>, тАШI am able neither to enjoy nor to abandonтАЩ, <ls>┼Ъak. v, 18</ls>; <s>na pUrvA<srs />hRe na ca parA<srs />hRe</s>, тАШneither in the forenoon nor in the afternoonтАЩ);
